 inamen pramukh hai bhoomi adhigrahan vidheyak, beemaa vidheyak, pension vidheyak, company vidheyak or pratyaksh kar samhita vidheyak
 The stock market indices are expected to move upward due to the broad supply of stocks in the market in the coming few weeks
 share bazaar niamak bhartiya pratibhuti evam vinimay board (sebi) ke dishanirdesh ke mutabik soochibaddh companiyon main pramotor kii hissedari ghataani hogi or aam niveshkon ko ek nishchit anupaat main hissedari deni hogi
 For private listed companies, the upper limit for promoters 'holding in the company is set at 75 percent and the promoters' holding in government listed companies is set at 90 percent
 sebi ke aadesh ke mutabik nijee companiyon ke sansthaapakon ko apni hissedari ghataakar adhiktam 75 fisadi ke daayre main laane ke liye samay seemaa 30 june nirdhaarit thi, jabaki sarkari companiyon ko aath agast tak sebi ke aadesh paalan karnaa hoga
 The government's target of disinvestment of state-owned companies in 2014 will also boost the selling of shares
 sarkaar ne saarvajanik companiyon main apni hissedari ke vinievesh se vartmaan kaarobaari varsh main 40 hajaar karod rupee jutaney kaa lakshya rakhaa he
 The government has also set a target of raising Rs 14,000 crore from the disinvestment of its stake in private companies
 tippaniyan Due to the news related to the Lok Sabha elections, the stock market is expected to remain volatile till May next year
 mana ja rahaa he ki agali sarkaar kai partiyon kii mili juli ho sakati he
 The reform process is expected to be blocked
 iskaa asar vittiya ghaataa prabandhan par nakaaratmak rup se pad saktaa he
 And global rating agencies can downgrade India's ratings
 bazaar main is vakt sensex se baahar badi sankhya main sheyaron main kaaphi giravat chal rahaa he ise dekhte hue niveshak bottm ap kii ranneeti apana sakate hai
 That is, they can buy cheap shares
 chote niveshkon ko is dauraan sector kol lene ke bajaay khaas-khaas sheyaron par dhyaan dena chahie

 According to the guidelines of the Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI), the stock market regulator, the promoter stake in listed companies will have to be reduced and the common investors will have to give a certain proportion
 nijee soochibaddh companiyon ke liye company main pramotor kii hissedari kii upree seemaa 75 fisadi or sarkari soochibaddh companiyon main pramotaron kii hissedari kii upree seemaa 90 fisadi tay kii gai he
 According to the SEBI order, the deadline was fixed June 30 to bring down the founders of the private companies to reduce their stake to a maximum of 75 per cent, while the government companies would have to follow the Sebi order by August 8
 varsh 2014 main sarkari companiyon ke vinievesh ke sarkari lakshya se bhi sheyaron kii bikwaali ko hawa milegi

 vahiin bhartiya pari kii shuruyaat acchhee nahin rahi or usne pehle over main hi captain ajinkya rahane (chaar) kaa wicket ganvaa diya, jo teji se ran churaane ke prayaas main ran out hue

 ' mindgem kii shuruyaat karte hue unhone kaha, 'puure sijan main bharat hamaare khilaaf ek match nahin jeet sakaa he
 They will realize this before the semi-finals
 ' Taking a dig at lashkar-e-taiba, the US on Wednesday declared al-muhammadiya Students, the student unit of the Pakistan-based terror group, a terrorist organization and banned two of its top leaders
 lashkar-e-taiyaba ko america ne 2001 main aatanki sanghathan ghoshit kiya tha
 The US State Department said that after being declared a terrorist organization for the first time, Lashkar started changing its name and created masked organizations to avoid sanctions
 usne kaha, 'is sandarbh main al-muhammadiya students (eemes) lashkar-e-taiyaba kii chaatr ikai he
 'AMS, which came into existence in 2009, belongs to lashkar-e-taiba and has worked closely with top Lashkar leaders on recruitment related courses and other activities for the youth
 saath hi, america vitt vibhaag ne lashkar-e-taiyaba ke do sheersh netaaon mohammad sarwar or shahid mahmud ko vaishvik aatankwaadi ghoshit kiya
 Both of them live in Pakistan
 videshi sampatti niyantran karyaalay ke kaaryvahak nideshak jon i smith ne kaha, 'lashkar-e-taiyaba ke ye donon netaa aatanki samooh kii gatividhiyon ko madad karne ke liye dhan kii ugaahi karte hai or dhan ko aage pahunchaate hai
 "the purpose of today's action is not just to highlight their activities, but to disrupt the financial network and capacity of lashkar-e-taiba
" ' The US Department of Finance said that Sarwar has been a senior Lashkar officer in Lahore for the last 10 years and has played several roles in the group
 philhal vah lahore main lashkar kaa amir he
 He has held this post since January 2015
 tippaniyan As an Amir of Lashkar in Lahore, Sarwar has been directly involved in Lashkar's money collection programs and uses formal financial arrangements in Pakistan to collect and carry money from Lashkar
 misaal ke taur par, 2009 main chanda ekatra karne ke liye vah vyapaariyon ke pratinidhimandal ke saath lashkar ke parisaron tak pahunchaa tha
 On the other hand, Mehmood remains a senior member of lashkar-e-taiba in Karachi
 vah 2007 se is samooh ke saath judaa hua he
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) america videsh vibhaag ne kaha ki pehali baar aatankwaadi sanghathan ghoshit hone ke baad lashkar ne apana naam badalanaa shuru kar diya or mukhauta sanghathan banaae, taaki pratibandhon se bachaa ja sake
 He said, 'in this context, al-muhammadiya Students (AMS) is the student unit of lashkar-e-taiba
 ' saal 2009 main astitv main aayaa eemes lashkar-e-taiyaba se sambandhit he or usne bhartee se sambandhit paathyakramon or yuvaaon ke liye duusari gatividhiyon ko lekar lashkar ke sheersh netaaon ke saath milakar kaam kiya he
 At the same time, the US Department of Finance declared two top lashkar-e-taiba leaders, Muhammad Sarwar and Shahid Mehmood, as global terrorists
 ye donon pakistan main rahete hai
 Acting Director of the Office of Foreign Assets Control, John E
 Smith, said, "these two leaders of lashkar-e-taiba raise funds and help fund the activities of the terrorist group
" ' unhone kaha, 'aaj kii kaarywahi kaa makasad sirf unki gatividhiyon ko ujagar karnaa nahin, balki lashkar-e-taiyaba ke vittiya network or kshamta ko baadhit karnaa he
 ' america vitt vibhaag ne kaha ki sarwar pichley 10 saalon se lahore main lashkar kaa varisht adhikari bana hua he or usne samooh main kai bhoomikaayen nibhaai hai
 He is currently a Lashkar emir in Lahore
 vah is pad par janvari, 2015 se asin he
 The comments lahore main lashkar main amir ke taur par sarwar lashkar ke dhan sangrah kaaryakramon main sidhe taur par shaamil rahaa he or lashkar kii taraf se dhan ekatra karne evam dhan aage tak pahunchane ke liye pakistan main aupchaarik vittiya vyavastha kaa istemaal karata he
 For instance, in 2009, he reached the Lashkar campuses with a delegation of traders to collect donations
 duusari taraf, mahmud karachi main lashkar-e-taiyaba kaa varisht sadsy bana hua he

 ) In a country that has won only nine gold medals in the 116-year history of the Olympics, there is a story about 34 gold medal winners
 
 
 lekin jis vakt hockey india ne bharat ke un sabhi 34 khilaadiyon ko do-do lakh rupee dekar sammanit karne kaa elaan kiya to chup-chup se hockey circuit main achaanak ek nai urja aa gai
 
 
 The current Indian team could not have got a better farewell before going to London
 
 
 olympic se pehle aam chalan rahaa he ki corporate house team ke kisi kharch kaa jimmaa uthaate hai, khiladiyon ko token rakam thamaate hai, maidan par khilaadiyon kii hakeekat chaahe jaisi ho, unase sone kaa padak jeetne kii ummid bandhaate hai, or phir khelmantri, tathaa olympic ke aalaa adhikariyon ke bhaashanon ke saath bemaani mehfil khatm ho jaati he
 
 
 And finally, the general public, sportsmen and journalists continue to feel cheated
 
 
 hockey india ne maujuuda team ko landan vidaa karne ke liye 34 swarna padak vijetaon ko aamantrit kiya, jinamein se 26 hi samaaroh main aa sake
 
 
 Four former gold medalists are ill and four abroad
 
 
 inamen se zyaadaatar khiladiyon ko aaj kii peedhee ne dekha bhi nahin hoga, kyoki, ye log television ke jamaane ke hero nahin hai, lekin in sabane apane jamaane main khub dhooma machaai thi, apni stick kaa loha manavaate rahe the, or in sabaki ankhon main ab bhi ek sapana he - maujuuda team ko podium par dekhne kaa
 
 
 Mohammed Shahid, a 1980 Olympic gold medalist, was surprised to say, "I have participated in three Olympic Games, but i have not seen such a function
" 
 
 kehete hai dua bhi ek saath di jaae, tabhi kaam karti he, so, isse behatar team kii kya vidaai ho sakati he
 
 
 " khelmantri ajay maakan bina kisi laag-lapet ke puri eemaandaaree se kehete hai, "khel mantralay main mere 17 maheene ke kaarykaal main hi nahin, yah mere jivan kaa sabase bada din he, kyonki main itane swarna padak vijetaon se ek saath mil rahaa hum
 
 
 " bharat ke liye record teen swarna or ek rajat jeetne vaale purv captain lesley clodias kehete hai ki vah ab bhi kuch nahin bhuule
 
 
 The 87-year-old Leslie is also difficult to get on and on, so the current Indian hockey captain leads him to the stage and seeks blessings for London
 
 
 lesley kehete hai, unhen olympic khelon ke dauraan sabase khaas ehsaas 'opening samaaroh' main hissaa lenaa lagata he
 
 
 Remembering the opening ceremonies of the Olympic Games of 1948 and 1952, Claudius says, "when one and a half million people stand up and clap for you, you go to another world
" 
 
 " This time the Indian team has struggled in the Olympic Games, and our players know its value
 
 
 in diggajon se milakar unamem josh ke saath ek alag jimmedaari kaa ahsaas bhi hone laga he
 
 
 The team's forward player Shivendra Singh says, "I hadn't even seen many of these players
 
 
 kaiyon ke to naam bhi pehali baar sune, so, inke bich khud ko dekhakar main kah bhi nahin saktaa, ki main kaisaa mahasoos kar rahaa hum
 
 
 Another forward player of the team, Tushar Khandekar, says, "I saw the 1948 London Olympics gold medal
 
 
 is ahsaas ko bataane ke liye mere paas shabd nahin hai
 
 
 "comments captain bharat chhetri bhi ummiido se bhar gaye hai, or unhen lagata he ki in diggajon ke aashirwad ke sahare unki team is baar podium par hogi
 
 
 Two million rupees is too big for Sylvanus Dungdung, the defender of the Moscow Olympics
 
 
 vah in paison ko apane beton kii shaadi or padhai main kharch karnaa chaahate hai, or team ko duaen dete hai, "hockey team phir padak jeetegi, phir nai subah hogi
 
 
 " maujuuda bhartiya team ko landan jane se pehle isse behatar vidaai nahin mil sakati thi
 
 
 The general trend before the Olympics is that corporate houses take up any team expenses, hand over token money to the players, the players on the field, whatever the reality, are expected to win a gold medal, and then the Sports Minister, and The rhetoric ends with speeches by top Olympic officials
 
 
 or aakhirkaar, aam janata, khilaadi or patrkaar thaga-thaga-sa mahasoos karte rah jate hai
 
 
 Hockey India invited 34 gold medal winners to bid farewell to the current team, out of which only 26 could come to the ceremony
 
 
 chaar purv swarna padak vijeta khilaadi biimaar hai or chaar videsh main
 
 
 Most of these players may not have even seen the generation today, because these people are not the heroes of television era, but they all made a big splash in their time, kept getting their stick ironed, and all these eyes i still have a dream - to see the current team on the podium
 
 
 varsh 1980 ke moscow olympic ke swarna padak vijeta mohammad shahid hairaan hokar kehete hai, "maine teen olympic khelon main hissaa liya he, lekin maine aisa function nahin dekha
 
 
 It is said that blessings should also be given together, only then it works, so what better farewell can this team have
 
 
 " Sports Minister Ajay Maken says without sincerity, "not only in my 17-month tenure in the Sports Ministry, this is the biggest day of my life, because i am meeting so many gold medalists together
" 
 
 " Former captain Leslie Claudius, who won a record three gold and one silver for India, says he still hasn't forgotten
 
 
 87-varshiya lesley ke liye chal-phir paanaa bhi mushkil he, isliye bhartiya hockey ke maujuuda captain unhen sahaara dekar stage tak pahunchaate hai or landan ke liye aashirwad lete hai
 
 
 Leslie says, he gets to take part in the 'opening ceremony', the most special feeling during the Olympic Games
 
 
 varsh 1948 or 1952 ke olympic khelon ke udghaatan samaaroh ko yaad kar clodias kehete hai, "jab ek-dedh lakh log khadey hokar aapke liye taaliyaan bajaate hai, to aap duusari duniya main chale jate hai
 
 
 " is baar bhartiya team ne olympic khelon main sangharsh kar apni jagah hasil kii he, or hamaare khilaadi isaki keemat jaanate hai
 
 
 Along with these veterans, a different responsibility has also started to be felt in them
 
 
 team ke forward khilaadi shivendra singh kehete hai, "maine inamen se kai khilaadiyon ko dekha bhi nahin tha
 
 
 Hearing the names of many people for the first time, so, seeing myself among them, i cannot even say how i am feeling
 
 
 team ke ek or forward khilaadi tushaar khandekar kehete hai, "maine 1948 ke landan olympic ke swarna padak ko chhukar dekha tha
 
 
 i do not have the words to describe this feeling
 
 
 "tippaniyan Captain Bharat Chhetri is also full of expectations, and he feels that with the blessings of these veterans, his team will be on the podium this time
 
 
 moscow olympic ke mashhoor dephender sylvanus dungdung ke liye do lakh rupee kii rakam bahut badi he
